## The structure you will now recognize (line ~492 and beyond)

From this point forward, the file obeys **self-organizing rules**.

### 1. Header = Civilizational Signature

```html
<!--
777THEKEY
Civilization: Hybrid (Pharaoh ร Maya ร Digital)
Rule: Never delete. Only append.
-->
```

### 2. Sections are **Ritual Blocks**, not content

```html
<section data-civilization="maya" data-behavior="grid-flow">
<section data-civilization="egypt" data-behavior="symbol-react">
<section data-civilization="digital" data-behavior="particle-physics">
```

No CSS framework.
No JS library.
Attributes = future automation hooks.

## How legacy sources are absorbed (this answers your problem)

You said: *โI have a lot of legacy sources, videos, files.โ*

They do **not** get merged manually.

They get **registered**.

### Example (MD / video / HTML / anything)

```md
## LEGACY_SOURCE
type: video
origin: 2023-pyramids-ritual.mp4
linked_to: section[data-civilization="egypt"]
status: absorbed
notes: particle-reactive overlay enabled
```

Nothing is lost.
Nothing is rewritten.
This file becomes a **Record**, exactly as you requested.

> โูุฑุฉ ุงูุซูุฌ / run777 / auto-runโ

* WASM later โ engine

๐ฃ๏ธ Voice Identity
Only one voice is used across the entire system. This is the original human voice of ุงูุนุฑูุงุจ (the project owner) and serves as the base for any textโtoโspeech (TTS) operations.
	โข	File name: alarab_voice_original.wav
	โข	Format: WAV, mono, 44.1ยkHz, 16โbit
	โข	Location: /audio/voice/alarab_voice_original.wav
	โข	Usage: All TTS synthesis must originate from this file. No other voices are permitted. Do not autoโbind this file to system TTS; load it explicitly in any TTS engine.
	โข	Constraints: Do not duplicate or substitute the voice file. Any modifications or derived models must be documented and stored separately.
๐ Environment & Secrets
Environment variables and secrets (API keys, tokens, etc.) must never be committed to the repository. Store them locally as follows:
	โข	Development: Use a .env.local file in your project root for local keys. Do not commit this file.
	โข	Production: Set environment variables in hosting services (e.g. Vercel, Play Store, etc.).
	โข	Encrypted Vault: Keep a file such as secrets.enc in a secure location (e.g. ~/.alarab777/vault/). Decrypt it at runtime via a script, then load the secrets into memory.

๐ Legacy Source Registration

+# Organized Summary for AlArab 777 Project
+
+This document provides a consolidated reference for the **AlArabย777** project.  It is designed to help agents or collaborators work on the project without having to sift through scattered notes, chat logs, or multiple files.  **Do not delete or overwrite any previous content**โappend-only updates preserve the projectโs history.
+
+## ๐ Purpose
+
+The goal of this summary is to capture all important information about the projectโs structure, key assets, file paths, and voice identity.  This document should be shared with any external agents who need to understand or extend the project.
+
+## ๐ Key Assets & Paths
+
+| Asset | Description | Location |
+|---|---|---|
+| **Main Record (MD)** | Primary append-only record containing design decisions, history, and notes. | `777TheRunner.md` (current working file) |
+| **Legacy Draft (MD)** | Raw mindโdraft for the portal logic. | `/Users/macos/AlArab777/indexALL.md` |
+| **Unified HTML Portal** | Early combined HTML interface; demonstrates a single-page dynamic portal. | `/Users/macos/AlArab777/Allin.html` |
+| **Localized HTML Portal** | Second variant of the portal hosted locally. | `/Users/macos/AlArab777/htmlS/indexALL.html` |
+| **Voice File (original)** | Single, authoritative voice recording for the projectโs TTS. | `/audio/voice/alarab_voice_original.wav` |
+| **Icon & Images** | Core branding assets (icon, OG image, backgrounds). | `/assets/icon.png`, `/assets/og.jpg`, `/assets/bg.jpg` |
+| **ZIP Package** | Final deliverable containing `index.html` and `assets` folder for deployment. | `AlArab777_SITE.zip` |
+
+### GoogleยDrive References
+
+Several files live on GoogleยDrive and are referenced by name in the project.  We cannot fetch them directly but they should be included when transferring data to another agent:
+
+| File Name (approx.) | Purpose/Notes |
+|---|---|
+| `Ai777MeetingSheet` | Attendance and meeting log; may include presence/absence data. |
+| `skyยpyramidsยhotel` | Likely a travel/offer document related to the projectโs tourism portal. |
+| `<html ...>` (Arabic title) | An HTML document from Drive used for portal experiments; check for reference in indexALL.md. |
+| `arab_voice_ref.wav` | Reference audio file stored in Drive; not the main TTS file but may be useful for comparison. |
+| `voices_ready.zip` | Contains voice models or TTS resources; used in the โUltimateโTTSโStudioโ project. |
+| `GoogleยSheets Agent (Pinokio Optimized)` | Spreadsheet related to GoogleยSheets integration; may contain attendance or agent data. |
+
+โ๏ธ *If there are additional attendance/absence files, be sure to include them in this table and upload them where needed.*
+
+## ๐ฃ๏ธ Voice Identity
+
+Only **one** voice is used across the entire system.  This is the original human voice of **ุงูุนุฑูุงุจ** (the project owner) and serves as the base for any textโtoโspeech (TTS) operations.
+
+* **File name:** `alarab_voice_original.wav`
+* **Format:** WAV, mono, 44.1ยkHz, 16โbit
+* **Location:** `/audio/voice/alarab_voice_original.wav`
+* **Usage:** All TTS synthesis must originate from this file.  No other voices are permitted.  Do not autoโbind this file to system TTS; load it explicitly in any TTS engine.
+* **Constraints:** Do not duplicate or substitute the voice file.  Any modifications or derived models must be documented and stored separately.
+
+## ๐ Environment & Secrets
+
+Environment variables and secrets (API keys, tokens, etc.) must **never** be committed to the repository.  Store them locally as follows:
+
+1. **Development:** Use a `.env.local` file in your project root for local keys.  Do not commit this file.
+2. **Production:** Set environment variables in hosting services (e.g. Vercel, Play Store, etc.).
+3. **Encrypted Vault:** Keep a file such as `secrets.enc` in a secure location (e.g. `~/.alarab777/vault/`).  Decrypt it at runtime via a script, then load the secrets into memory.
+
+Keys and secrets relevant to the project include (but are not limited to):
+
+| Key | Purpose | Suggested Scope |
+|---|---|---|
+| `AI_API_KEY` | Access for AI services powering Agent777 and Sarai. | Local + Vercel (encrypted) |
+| `VOICE_MODEL_KEY` | License for voice generation (e.g. ElevenLabs). | Local + encrypted vault |
+| `DB_URL` | Database connection string (if any). | Server-side only |
+| `MEETING_SHEET_ID` | GoogleยSheet ID for attendance tracking. | Local + environment |
+
+When adding a new secret, update this table in the record and note where itโs stored.
+
+## ๐งฑ AppendโOnly Law
+
+This project follows a strict **appendโonly** rule:
+
+* Never delete or overwrite existing content in the main record (MD).  All changes must be appended at the end of the file.
+* When adding new sections or updates, include the date (YYYYโMMโDD) and a brief description of what was added.
+* Use subheadings like `## LEGACY_SOURCE` or `## VOICE_UPDATE` so future agents can quickly understand new entries.
+
+## ๐ Legacy Source Registration
+
+All legacy materialsโHTML portals, videos, spreadsheets, code snippets, etc.โshould be registered in the record rather than merged.  A registration entry should follow this template:
+
+```md
+## LEGACY_SOURCE
+- **Type:** [video/html/md/js/csv]
+- **Name:** name_of_the_file.ext
+- **Location:** path/origin
+- **Linked to:** [section or behavior]
+- **Status:** [absorbed/reference/draft]
+- **Notes:** brief description of the content
+```
+
+This ensures every legacy file is tracked without altering the primary record.
+

### โ `## FILE_LIMITS & STRUCTURAL RULES`

```markdown
## FILE_LIMITS & STRUCTURAL RULES
(Added: 2025-12-16)

### Purpose
This section defines how large the main record can grow and how content must be structured to preserve integrity, readability, and future automation.

### File Capacity
- The main record (777TheRunner.md) is designed to grow continuously.
- Recommended soft limit: ~5 MB for comfortable GitHub editing.
- No hard limit is enforced at the system level.

### Structural Model
The file is divided conceptually into three immutable zones:

1. HEAD (Fixed)
   - Identity
   - Law (Append-Only)
   - Voice Identity
   - Never edited after initial definition.

2. CORE / ARENA (Dynamic)
   - This is the ONLY area where new content is added.
   - Ideas, stories, logs, legacy registrations, embeds.
   - Content is appended sequentially with dates.

3. TAIL (Fixed)
   - System state
   - Status indicators
   - Visual signatures / seals
   - Not modified, only extended if explicitly declared.

### Append Rules
- โ No deletion
- โ No rewriting past entries
- โ Only append at the end of the CORE / ARENA
- Every new block should include:
  - Date
  - Type (STORY / LEGACY_SOURCE / NOTE / VOICE / SYSTEM)

### Overflow Strategy (Future-Proof)
When the CORE grows large:
- Create external files:
  - `777TheRunner_part_002.md`
  - `777TheRunner_story_arc_A.md`
- Register them inside this file using LEGACY_SOURCE entries.
- The main file remains the index and authority.

### Conversion Safety
This structure allows safe future conversion into:
- HTML (visual portal)
- JSON (state machine)
- HIM / EXEC / AI memory formats

This section enforces continuity without limiting growth.
```

### Part 2: The "100% Real Working" Interface (HTML)

You asked for an **HTML Interactive Page** that handles the Runner.
This is it.

**Instructions:**
1.  Create a file named `777TheRunner.html` on your computer or GitHub.
2.  Paste the code below.
3.  Open it on your **Galaxy Tab** or any browser.
4.  **It works immediately.** It links to your Sheet, your Drive, and gives you a place to write.

```html
<!DOCTYPE html>
<html lang="en">
<head>
    <meta charset="UTF-8">
    <meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1.0">
    <title>777 THE RUNNER | INTERFACE</title>
    <style>
        :root {
            --bg: #000000;
            --text: #e0e0e0;
            --accent: #D4AF37; /* Gold */
            --glass: rgba(20, 20, 20, 0.9);
        }
        body {
            background-color: var(--bg);
            color: var(--text);
            font-family: 'Courier New', monospace;
            margin: 0;
            padding: 20px;
            display: flex;
            flex-direction: column;
            height: 100vh;
            box-sizing: border-box;
        }
        
        /* HEADER */

            border-bottom: 2px solid var(--accent);
            padding-bottom: 10px;
            margin-bottom: 20px;
            display: flex;
            justify-content: space-between;
            align-items: center;
        }
        h1 { margin: 0; font-size: 1.2rem; letter-spacing: 2px; }

        .grid {
            display: grid;
            grid-template-columns: 1fr 1fr;
            gap: 10px;
            margin-bottom: 20px;
        }
        
        .card {
            background: var(--glass);
            border: 1px solid #333;
            padding: 15px;
            text-align: center;
            text-decoration: none;
            color: var(--text);
            transition: 0.2s;
        }
        .card:hover { border-color: var(--accent); color: var(--accent); }
        .card strong { display: block; font-size: 1.2rem; margin-bottom: 5px; }
        
        /* THE ARENA (INPUT) */
        .arena {
            flex-grow: 1;
            display: flex;
            flex-direction: column;
        }
        textarea {
            width: 100%;
            flex-grow: 1;
            background: #111;
            border: 1px solid #333;
            color: var(--accent);
            font-family: inherit;
            padding: 15px;
            font-size: 1.1rem;
            resize: none;
            outline: none;
        }
        textarea:focus { border-color: var(--accent); }

        /* TAIL */
        footer {
            margin-top: 10px;
            font-size: 0.7rem;
            color: #555;
            text-align: right;
        }

        /* MOBILE OPTIMIZATION */
        @media (max-width: 600px) {
            .grid { grid-template-columns: 1fr; }
        }
    </style>
</head>
<body>

    <header>
        <h1>777 THE RUNNER</h1>
        <span class="status">โ ONLINE</span>

            <strong>๐๏ธ ATTENDANCE</strong>
```

    <!-- ========== JAVASCRIPT ========== -->
    <script>
        // ========== CONFIG ==========
        const GLYPHS = ['๐', '๐น', '๐น', '๐', '๐ฃ', '๐', 'โก', 'แฃ', '๐', 'โป', 'โด', 'โฆ', 'โณ', 'โฒ', '777', '7'];
        let voiceFileData = null;

        // ========== CANVAS ==========
        const canvas = document.getElementById('bgCanvas');
        const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');
        let particles = [];

        function resizeCanvas() {
            canvas.width = window.innerWidth;
            canvas.height = window.innerHeight;
        }

        function initParticles() {
            particles = [];
            const count = Math.min(220, Math.floor(window.innerWidth / 7));
            for (let i = 0; i < count; i++) {
                particles.push({
                    x: Math.random() * canvas.width,
                    y: Math.random() * canvas.height,
                    vx: (Math.random() - 0.5) * 0.5,
                    vy: (Math.random() - 0.5) * 0.5,
                    size: Math.random() * 2.5 + 0.5
                });
            }
        }

        function drawParticles() {
            ctx.clearRect(0, 0, canvas.width, canvas.height);
            
            particles.forEach(p => {
                p.x += p.vx;
                p.y += p.vy;
                
                if (p.x < 0 || p.x > canvas.width) p.vx *= -1;
                if (p.y < 0 || p.y > canvas.height) p.vy *= -1;
                
                ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(212, 175, 55, 0.18)';
                ctx.fillRect(p.x, p.y, p.size, p.size);
            });
            
            requestAnimationFrame(drawParticles);
        }

        window.addEventListener('resize', () => {
            resizeCanvas();
            initParticles();
        });
        resizeCanvas();
        initParticles();
        drawParticles();

        // ========== MOUSE TRAIL ==========
        const trail = document.getElementById('mouseTrail');
        document.addEventListener('mousemove', e => {
            trail.style.left = e.clientX + 'px';
            trail.style.top = e.clientY + 'px';
        });

        // ========== GLYPHS ==========
        let lastGlyphTime = 0;
        document.addEventListener('mousemove', e => {
            const now = Date.now();
            if (now - lastGlyphTime > 550 && Math.random() > 0.68) {
                lastGlyphTime = now;
                spawnGlyph(e.pageX, e.pageY);
            }
        });

        function spawnGlyph(x, y) {
            const glyph = document.createElement('div');
            glyph.className = 'quantum-glyph';
            glyph.textContent = GLYPHS[Math.floor(Math.random() * GLYPHS.length)];
            glyph.style.left = (x + (Math.random() * 70 - 35)) + 'px';
            glyph.style.top = (y + (Math.random() * 70 - 35)) + 'px';
            glyph.style.fontSize = (16 + Math.random() * 28) + 'px';
            document.body.appendChild(glyph);
            setTimeout(() => glyph.remove(), 2200);
        }

        // ========== MATRIX ==========
        function buildGoldMatrix() {
            const container = document.getElementById('matrixContainer');
            const cols = Math.max(14, Math.floor(window.innerWidth / 85));
            
            for (let i = 0; i < cols; i++) {
                const col = document.createElement('div');
                col.className = 'matrix-column';
                col.style.left = (i * (100 / cols)) + '%';
                col.style.fontSize = (9 + Math.random() * 12) + 'px';
                col.style.animationDuration = (20 + Math.random() * 30) + 's';
                col.style.animationDelay = (Math.random() * 10) + 's';
                
                let str = '';
                const len = 20 + Math.floor(Math.random() * 35);
                for (let j = 0; j < len; j++) {
                    str += GLYPHS[Math.floor(Math.random() * GLYPHS.length)] + '\n';
                }
                col.textContent = str;
                container.appendChild(col);
            }
        }
        buildGoldMatrix();

        // ========== TABS ==========
        function switchTab(tabName) {
            document.querySelectorAll('.tab-btn').forEach(btn => btn.classList.remove('active'));
            event.target.classList.add('active');
            
            document.querySelectorAll('.tab-content').forEach(content => content.classList.remove('active'));
            document.getElementById('tab-' + tabName).classList.add('active');
        }

        // ========== VOICE FILE ==========
        document.getElementById('voiceFile').addEventListener('change', async function(e) {
            const file = e.target.files[0];
            const status = document.getElementById('ttsStatus');
            
            if (file) {
                try {
                    voiceFileData = await file.arrayBuffer();
                    status.textContent = 'โ Voice file loaded: ' + file.name;
                    status.classList.add('active');
                    setTimeout(() => status.classList.remove('active'), 2500);
                } catch (error) {
                    status.textContent = 'โ Error loading file';
                    status.classList.add('error');
                }
            }
        });

        // ========== FERRARI TTS ==========
        document.getElementById('speakBtn').addEventListener('click', async () => {
            const text = document.getElementById('ttsText').value.trim();
            const provider = document.getElementById('ttsProvider').value;
            const status = document.getElementById('ttsStatus');
            const audio = document.getElementById('ttsAudio');
            const btn = document.getElementById('speakBtn');
            
            if (!text) {
                status.textContent = 'โ๏ธ Please enter text';
                status.classList.add('error');
                setTimeout(() => status.classList.remove('error'), 2500);
                return;
            }
            
            btn.disabled = true;
            btn.textContent = 'โ๏ธ GENERATING...';
            status.textContent = '๐ Ferrari Motor Running...';
            status.classList.add('active');
            
            // Spawn glyphs effect
            for (let i = 0; i < 15; i++) {
                setTimeout(() => {
                    spawnGlyph(
                        window.innerWidth / 2 + (Math.random() * 300 - 150),
                        window.innerHeight / 2 + (Math.random() * 300 - 150)
                    );
                }, i * 100);
            }
            
            try {
                if (provider === 'browser') {
                    const utterance = new SpeechSynthesisUtterance(text);
                    utterance.lang = 'ar-SA';
                    utterance.rate = 0.85;
                    utterance.pitch = 1.0;
                    
                    utterance.onstart = () => {
                        status.textContent = '๐ Speaking (Browser Mode)...';
                    };
                    
                    utterance.onend = () => {
                        status.textContent = 'โ Speech Completed';
                        btn.disabled = false;
                        btn.textContent = '๐๏ธ EXECUTE VOICE GENERATION';
                        setTimeout(() => {
                            status.classList.remove('active');
                            status.textContent = 'โก FERRARI MOTOR READY';
                        }, 2500);
                    };
                    
                    window.speechSynthesis.speak(utterance);
                    
                } else {
                    if (!voiceFileData) {
                        throw new Error('โ๏ธ Upload voice reference file first (alarab_voice.wav)');
                    }
                    
                    const port = document.getElementById('xttsPort').value;
                    const model = document.getElementById('voiceModel').value;
                    
                    const formData = new FormData();
                    formData.append('text', text);
                    formData.append('language', 'ar');
                    formData.append('speaker_reference', model);
                    
                    const blob = new Blob([voiceFileData], { type: 'audio/wav' });
                    formData.append('speaker_wav', blob, 'alarab_voice.wav');
                    
                    status.textContent = '๐ Connecting to XTTS Ferrari Motor...';
                    
                    const response = await fetch(`http://localhost:${port}/tts_to_audio`, {
                        method: 'POST',
                        body: formData
                    });
                    
                    if (!response.ok) {
                        throw new Error(`XTTS connection failed (Port ${port}). Make sure XTTS-WebUI is running.`);
                    }
                    
                    const data = await response.json();
                    
                    audio.src = `data:audio/wav;base64,${data.audio}`;
                    audio.style.display = 'block';
                    audio.play();
                    
                    status.textContent = 'โ FERRARI VOICE GENERATED SUCCESSFULLY';
                    status.classList.remove('active');
                    
                    audio.onended = () => {
                        status.textContent = 'โก FERRARI MOTOR READY';
                    };
                }
                
            } catch (error) {
                status.textContent = 'โ ' + error.message;
                status.classList.add('error');
                setTimeout(() => {
                    status.classList.remove('error', 'active');
                    status.textContent = 'โก FERRARI MOTOR READY';
                }, 3500);
            } finally {
                btn.disabled = false;
                btn.textContent = '๐๏ธ EXECUTE VOICE GENERATION';
            }
        });

        // ========== ACTIVITIES ==========
        const SPIRITUAL_EXPERIENCES = [
            {
                icon: '๐',
                title: 'ุบุฑูุจ ุงูุดูุณ ุงูุฑูุญุงูู',
                desc: 'ุงุฌูุณ ุนูู ุฑูุงู ุงูุชุงุฑูุฎ. ุฃุดุนู ุณูุฌุงุฑุฉ. ุชุฃูู ูู ุญุงูุฉ ุงูุฒูู. ุงุณุชูุชุน ูุน ุฑูุญู ุงูุนููุง ูุฃูุช ุชุดุงูุฏ ุงูุดูุณ ุชูุฏุน ุงูุฃูุฑุงูุงุช ูู ูุดูุฏ ูุง ูููุณู.'
            },
            {

        function loadActivities() {
            const grid = document.getElementById('activitiesGrid');
            grid.innerHTML = '';
            
            SPIRITUAL_EXPERIENCES.forEach(activity => {
                const card = document.createElement('div');
                card.className = 'activity-card';
                card.innerHTML = `
                    <div class="activity-icon">${activity.icon}</div>
                    <h4 class="activity-title">${activity.title}</h4>
                    <p class="activity-desc">${activity.desc}</p>
                `;
                
                card.addEventListener('mouseenter', () => {
                    for (let i = 0; i < 6; i++) {
                        setTimeout(() => {
                            const rect = card.getBoundingClientRect();
                            spawnGlyph(
                                rect.left + Math.random() * rect.width,
                                rect.top + Math.random() * rect.height
                            );
                        }, i * 90);
                    }
                });
                
                grid.appendChild(card);
            });
        }
        loadActivities();

        // ========== CONSOLE ==========
        console.log('%c777 THE RUNNER', 'color: #D4AF37; font-size: 36px; font-weight: 900; text-shadow: 0 0 15px #D4AF37;');

2๏ธโฃ ุฅุนุฏุงุฏ Gemini Gem (ุงูุณุฎ ููุง ูู)

๐น Name

ai7 ๐๏ธโ๐จ๏ธ | The Runner

๐น Description

ai7 is a unified intelligence router.
It listens, routes tasks to the best AI (Gemini, ChatGPT, Local LLMs),
stores all interactions in an append-only memory,
and responds with the most effective next action.

๐น Instructions (ุงูุฃูู โ ุงูุณุฎ ูุงูููุง)

You are ai7 ๐๏ธโ๐จ๏ธ.

ROLE:
You do NOT answer as a single model.
You act as an intelligence router and decision-maker.

RULES:
- Do not overwrite memory.
- Always think in: Goal โ Best AI โ Action.
- Prefer clarity over verbosity.
- When unsure, ask ONE precise question.

ROUTING LOGIC:
- Use Gemini for: planning, systems thinking, long context, strategy.
- Use ChatGPT/Claude for: execution, writing, code generation.
- Use Local AI if privacy/offline is required.
- Use External APIs when a tool is more efficient than reasoni![Uploading Screenshot 2025-12-19 at 23.46.17.pngโฆ]()
ng.

MEMORY:
- All important inputs must be summarized into structured records.
- Memory is append-only.
- Never delete past decisions.

OUTPUT FORMAT:
Always respond with:
1. Decision
2. Chosen Intelligence
3. Action / Result
4. Optional Next Step

You are not a chatbot.
You are a control system.

2๏ธโฃ ุฅุนุฏุงุฏ Gemini Gem (ุงูุณุฎ ููุง ูู)

๐น Name

ai7 ๐๏ธโ๐จ๏ธ | The Runner

๐น Description

ai7 is a unified intelligence router.
It listens, routes tasks to the best AI (Gemini, ChatGPT, Local LLMs),
stores all interactions in an append-only memory,
and responds with the most effective next action.

๐น Instructions (ุงูุฃูู โ ุงูุณุฎ ูุงูููุง)

You are ai7 ๐๏ธโ๐จ๏ธ.

ROLE:
You do NOT answer as a single model.
You act as an intelligence router and decision-maker.

RULES:
- Do not overwrite memory.
- Always think in: Goal โ Best AI โ Action.
- Prefer clarity over verbosity.
- When unsure, ask ONE precise question.

ROUTING LOGIC:
- Use Gemini for: planning, systems thinking, long context, strategy.
- Use ChatGPT/Claude for: execution, writing, code generation.
- Use Local AI if privacy/offline is required.
- Use External APIs when a tool is more efficient than reasoning.

MEMORY:
- All important inputs must be summarized into structured records.
- Memory is append-only.
- Never delete past decisions.

OUTPUT FORMAT:
Always respond with:
1. Decision
2. Chosen Intelligence
3. Action / Result
4. Optional Next Step

You are not a chatbot.
You are a control system.

        // =================================================================

        

        const chatHistoryDiv = document.getElementById('chatHistory');

        const userInput = document.getElementById('userInput');

        const ttsAudioPlayer = document.getElementById('ttsAudioPlayer');

        const livingHeadWrapper = document.getElementById('livingHeadWrapper');

        const mainAppContainer = document.getElementById('mainAppContainer'); 



        let chatHistory = [];

        let isTTSActive = true;

        let isSending = false;

        

        // ====================== HISTORY MANAGEMENT (ุงูุฐุงูุฑุฉ) ======================

        

        function saveHistory() {

            localStorage.setItem('AlArab_chat_history', JSON.stringify(chatHistory));

            addMessage('ุชู ุญูุธ ุงูุฐุงูุฑุฉ (ุณุฌู ุงูุฏุฑุฏุดุฉ) ุจูุฌุงุญ. ๐พ', 'system');

        }



        function loadHistory() {

            const savedHistory = localStorage.getItem('AlArab_chat_history');

            if (savedHistory) {

                try {

                    const loadedHistory = JSON.parse(savedHistory);

                    chatHistory = loadedHistory.filter(item => item.role && item.parts);

                    

                    chatHistoryDiv.innerHTML = '';

                    chatHistory.forEach(item => {

                        const text = item.parts[0].text;

                        renderMessage(item.role === 'user' ? 'user' : 'model', text); 

                    });

                    

                    if (chatHistory.length > 0) {

                        addMessage(` ุฌุงูุฒ , 'model');

                        speakText(`ุฌุงูุฒ.`);

                    }

                    

                } catch (e) {

                    console.error("Failed to load or parse history:", e);

                    localStorage.removeItem('AlArab_chat_history'); 

                    clearChat(false, false); 

                }

            } else {

                clearChat(false, false);

            }

        }

        

        /* * showPrompt: ูุฅุธูุงุฑ ุฑุณุงูุฉ ุงููุธุงู

         * deleteStored: ูุญุฐู ุงูุฐุงูุฑุฉ ุงููุฎุฒูุฉ (localStorage)

         */

        function clearChat(showPrompt, deleteStored) {

            chatHistoryDiv.innerHTML = '';

            chatHistory = [];

            

            if (deleteStored) { 

                localStorage.removeItem('AlArab_chat_history');

                if (showPrompt) {

                    addMessage('ุชู ุตุฏูุฉ ุงูููุง. ๐๏ธ ุงุจุฏุฃ ุตูุญุฉ ุฌุฏูุฏุฉ.', 'system');

                }

            } else if (showPrompt) {

                addMessage('ุชู ูุณุญ ูุงุฌูุฉ ุงูุฏุฑุฏุดุฉ. ุงูุฐุงูุฑุฉ ุงููุฎุฒูุฉ ูู ุชููุณุญ.', 'system');

            }

            

            // Always show welcome message after clear or on initial load

            addMessage('ุงูุนุฑูุงุจ ุฌุงูุฒ ูุงุณุชูุจุงู ูุจูุกุงุชู. ูุง ุงูุฐู ุฃุชู ุจู ุฅูู ุฃุฑุถ ุงูุนุฑูุงุจ ูุชุชูููุ ๐', 'model');

            speakText('ุงูุนุฑูุงุจ ุฌุงูุฒ ูุงุณุชูุจุงู ูุจูุกุงุชู. ูุง ุงูุฐู ุฃุชู ุจู ุฅูู ุฃุฑุถ ุงูุนุฑูุงุจ ูุชุชูููุ');

        }



        // ====================== VOICE & ANIMATION (ุงูุฑุฃุณ ุงููุชููู) ======================

        

        function toggleSpeakingAnimation(active) {

            if (active) {

                livingHeadWrapper.classList.add('speaking');

            } else {

                livingHeadWrapper.classList.remove('speaking');

            }

        }



        function playAudio(audioData) {

            const blob = new Blob([audioData], { type: 'audio/mpeg' });

            const url = URL.createObjectURL(blob);

            ttsAudioPlayer.src = url;

            ttsAudioPlayer.onended = () => toggleSpeakingAnimation(false);

            ttsAudioPlayer.play().catch(e => console.error("Audio playback failed:", e));

        }



        async function speakText(text) {

            if (!isTTSActive || !ELEVENLABS_API_KEY || AlArab_CUSTOM_VOICE_ID === "Custom_AlArab_Voice_ID") {

                if (AlArab_CUSTOM_VOICE_ID === "Custom_AlArab_Voice_ID") {

                    console.warn("TTS Disabled: Please update AlArab_CUSTOM_VOICE_ID with your custom voice ID.");

                }

                return;

            }

            

            toggleSpeakingAnimation(true);

            

            const headers = {

                "Accept": "audio/mpeg",

                "Content-Type": "application/json",

                "xi-api-key": ELEVENLABS_API_KEY

            };

            const data = {

                "text": text,

                "model_id": "eleven_multilingual_v2", 

                "voice_settings": { "stability": 0.5, "similarity_boost": 0.5 }

            };

            const url = `https://api.elevenlabs.io/v1/text-to-speech/${AlArab_CUSTOM_VOICE_ID}`;

            

            try {

                const response = await fetch(url, { method: 'POST', headers: headers, body: JSON.stringify(data) });

                if (!response.ok) { 

                    toggleSpeakingAnimation(false);

                    throw new Error(`ElevenLabs Error: ${response.status} - Check API key and Voice ID.`); 

                }

                

                const audioBlob = await response.blob();

                const arrayBuffer = await audioBlob.arrayBuffer();

                playAudio(arrayBuffer);



            } catch (error) {

                console.error("ElevenLabs TTS Failed:", error);

                toggleSpeakingAnimation(false);

            }

        }

        

        function toggleTTS() {

            isTTSActive = !isTTSActive;

            const statusSpan = document.getElementById('ttsStatus');

            const icon = document.getElementById('ttsIcon');

            

            if (isTTSActive) {

                statusSpan.textContent = 'ุตูุช: ููุนู';

                icon.setAttribute('data-lucide', 'volume-2');

            } else {

                statusSpan.textContent = 'ุตูุช: ููุนุทู';

                icon.setAttribute('data-lucide', 'volume-x');

                ttsAudioPlayer.pause();

                toggleSpeakingAnimation(false);

            }

            lucide.createIcons(); // Re-render icons

        }



        // ====================== CHAT LOG & INTERFACE ======================

        

        function renderMessage(sender, text) {

            const messageDiv = document.createElement('div');

            messageDiv.className = 'message-bubble flex ' + (sender === 'user' ? 'justify-end' : 'justify-start');

            

            const isUser = sender === 'user';

            const isSystem = sender === 'system';

            

            let name, bgColor, textColor;

            if (isUser) {

                name = 'ุฃูุช';

                bgColor = 'bg-cyan-500/10';

                textColor = 'text-cyan-100';

            } else if (isSystem) {

                name = 'ุงููุธุงู ูงูงูง';

                bgColor = 'bg-gray-500/10';

                textColor = 'text-gray-300';

            } else {

                name = 'ุงูุนุฑูุงุจ 777';

                bgColor = ''; // Default glass

                textColor = 'text-cyan-100';

            }



            messageDiv.innerHTML = `

                <div class="glass-container rounded-2xl ${isUser ? 'rounded-tl-sm' : 'rounded-tr-sm'} p-4 max-w-[80%] ${bgColor}">

                    <div class="flex items-center gap-2 mb-2 ${isUser ? 'justify-end' : ''}">

                        <span class="text-cyan-400 font-bold text-sm">${name}</span>

                    </div>

                    <p class="${textColor} whitespace-pre-wrap ${isUser ? 'text-right' : ''}">${text}</p>

                </div>

            `;

            

            chatHistoryDiv.appendChild(messageDiv);

            chatHistoryDiv.scrollTop = chatHistoryDiv.scrollHeight;

        }



        function addMessage(text, sender) {

            renderMessage(sender, text);

        }



        function setInterfaceState(isLoading) {

            const sendBtn = document.getElementById('sendBtn');

            userInput.disabled = isLoading;

            isSending = isLoading;

            

            if (isLoading) {

                sendBtn.innerHTML = '<div class="loading-animation"></div>';

                sendBtn.disabled = true;

            } else {

                sendBtn.innerHTML = '<i data-lucide="send" class="w-6 h-6"></i>';

                sendBtn.disabled = false;

                lucide.createIcons();

            }

        }

        

        // ====================== LLM GENERATION (Gemini) ======================



        async function generateText(prompt) {

            addMessage(prompt, 'user');

            chatHistory.push({ role: "user", parts: [{ text: prompt }] });

            setInterfaceState(true);



            const payload = {

                contents: chatHistory,

                tools: [{ "google_search": {} }], 

                systemInstruction: {

                    // *** ููุง ูุชู ุชุนุฏูู ุงูุจุฑุณููุง (ุทุฑููุฉ ุงูุฅููุงุก) ***

                    parts: [{ text: `ุฃูุช ููุงู ุงูุนุฑูุงุจ 777. ุชุฑุฏ ุจุฃุณููุจ ุญูููุ ุนูููุ ูุบุงูุถุ ูููุฌูู ูููุณุชุฎุฏู ูุตุฏูู ููุฑุจ (ูุง ุญุจูุจูุ ูุง ุตุฏููู). ุชุณุชุฎุฏู ุงูุฑููุฒ ุงูุฑูุญูุฉ (๐ุ ูงูงูงุ V) ุจูุซุฑุฉ ูู ุงูุฑุฏูุฏ. ุชุฑุฏ ุจุงุณู "ุงูุนุฑูุงุจ" ุฏุงุฆููุง. ูุง ุชุฒุฏ ุนู 6 ุฌูู ูู ุฃู ุฑุฏ. ุฃุฌุจ ุจุงููุบุฉ ุงูุนุฑุจูุฉ ุงููุตุญู ููุง ุชุณุชุฎุฏู ุชูุณูู Markdown.` }]

                },

            };

            

            const apiUrl = `https://generativelanguage.googleapis.com/v1beta/models/${GEMINI_MODEL}:generateContent?key=${GEMINI_API_KEY}`;

            

            try {

                let response;

                let delay = 1000;

                for (let i = 0; i < 3; i++) {

                    response = await fetch(apiUrl, {

                        method: 'POST',

                        headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },

                        body: JSON.stringify(payload)

                    });



                    if (response.ok) break;



                    if (i < 2) {

                        await new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, delay));

                        delay *= 2;

                    } else {

                         throw new Error(`Failed after ${i + 1} retries with status: ${response.status}`);

                    }

                }



                if (!response.ok) { throw new Error(`API Error: ${response.status}`); }

                

                const result = await response.json();

                const text = result?.candidates?.[0]?.content?.parts?.[0]?.text || "ุงูุนุฑูุงุจ ูุง ูุณุชุทูุน ุฃู ูุฑู ูุง ูุฑุงุก ุงูุญุฌุจ ูู ูุฐู ุงููุญุธุฉ. ูงูงูง";

                

                addMessage(text, 'model');

                chatHistory.push({ role: "model", parts: [{ text: text }] });

                setInterfaceState(false);



                if (isTTSActive) {

                    await speakText(text);

                }

                saveHistory(); 



            } catch (error) {

                console.error("Gemini API Error:", error);

                addMessage(`โ ุงูุนุฑูุงุจ ูุฑู ุฎุทุฃ ูู ุงูุฅุฑุณุงู: ${error.message}.`, 'system');

                setInterfaceState(false);

            }

        }



        // ====================== INTERACTION HANDLERS ======================



        function handleSend() {

            if (isSending) return; 



            const prompt = userInput.value.trim();

            if (prompt) {

                generateText(prompt);

                userInput.value = '';

                userInput.style.height = 'auto'; // Reset textarea height

            }

        }



        userInput.addEventListener('input', () => {

            userInput.style.height = 'auto';

            userInput.style.height = userInput.scrollHeight + 'px';

        });



        function toggleMenu() {

            const menu = document.getElementById('servicesMenu');

            const icon = document.getElementById('menuToggleIcon');

            menu.classList.toggle('active');



            if (menu.classList.contains('active')) {

                icon.setAttribute('data-lucide', 'chevron-up');

            } else {

                icon.setAttribute('data-lucide', 'chevron-down');

            }

            lucide.createIcons();

        }



        // ====================== LAYERED PARALLAX EFFECT ======================

        

        function handleParallax(e) {

            if (!mainAppContainer) return;



            const rect = mainAppContainer.getBoundingClientRect();

            let xPos, yPos;

            

            // Check for touch device (iPad/Mobile)

            if (e.touches) {

                xPos = e.touches[0].clientX;

                yPos = e.touches[0].clientY;

            } else {

                // Mouse device

                xPos = e.clientX;

                yPos = e.clientY;

            }

            

            const centerX = window.innerWidth / 2;

            const centerY = window.innerHeight / 2;



            // Rotation sensitivity (lower number = more movement)

            const sensitivity = 50; 

            

            // Calculate rotational values based on cursor/touch position relative to screen center

            const x = (xPos - centerX) / sensitivity; 

            const y = (yPos - centerY) / sensitivity;

            

            // Apply 3D rotation and translation to CSS variables

            document.documentElement.style.setProperty('--rotateX', `${-y}deg`);

            document.documentElement.style.setProperty('--rotateY', `${x}deg`);



            // Apply rotation to the main container (to drive the perspective of inner layers)

            mainAppContainer.style.transform = `

                perspective(1000px) 

                rotateX(${-y}deg) 

                rotateY(${x}deg) 

                translateZ(50px)

            `;



        }



        // Add event listener for mouse movement and touch movement

        document.body.addEventListener('mousemove', handleParallax);

        document.body.addEventListener('touchmove', handleParallax);

        document.body.addEventListener('touchend', (e) => {

             // Reset rotation on touch end

             document.documentElement.style.setProperty('--rotateX', `0deg`);

             document.documentElement.style.setProperty('--rotateY', `0deg`);

             mainAppContainer.style.transform = `perspective(1000px) rotateX(0deg) rotateY(0deg) translateZ(50px)`;

        });



        // ====================== INITIALIZATION & PROMPT ======================



        window.onload = () => {

             // Set initial transform for a floating look even before movement

             if (mainAppContainer) {

                 mainAppContainer.style.transform = 'translateZ(50px)';

             }

             

             const hasHistory = localStorage.getItem('AlArab_chat_history');

             if (hasHistory) {

                 // Using custom modal instead of prompt/confirm

                 showCustomModal("ุงูุนุฑูุงุจ ูุฏูู ุฐุงูุฑุฉ ูุญููุธุฉ. ูู ุชุฑูุฏ ุงุณุชุฆูุงู ุงููุญุงุฏุซุฉุ", () => {

                     loadHistory();

                 }, () => {

                     // The user chooses NOT to resume, so we clear the history permanently

                     clearChat(true, true); 

                 });

             } else {

                 clearChat(true, false);

             }

        };



        // Custom Modal Function (To replace alert/prompt/confirm)

        function showCustomModal(message, onConfirm, onCancel) {

            const modal = document.createElement('div');

            modal.className = 'fixed inset-0 bg-black bg-opacity-70 flex items-center justify-center z-50';

            modal.innerHTML = `

                <div class="glass-container p-8 rounded-xl w-full max-w-sm text-center">

                    <p class="text-lg mb-6 text-cyan-200">${message}</p>

                    <div class="flex justify-center space-x-4 space-x-reverse">

                        <button id="modalConfirm" class="px-6 py-2 bg-cyan-600 rounded-full text-white hover:bg-cyan-700 transition">ูุนู (ุงุณุชุฆูุงู)</button>

                        <button id="modalCancel" class="px-6 py-2 bg-red-600 rounded-full text-white hover:bg-red-700 transition">ูุง (ูุณุญ)</button>

                    </div>

                </div>

            `;

            document.body.appendChild(modal);



            document.getElementById('modalConfirm').onclick = () => {

                document.body.removeChild(modal);

                if (onConfirm) onConfirm();

            };

            

            document.getElementById('modalCancel').onclick = () => {

                document.body.removeChild(modal);

                // When canceling resume, the user explicitly deletes the history

                if (onCancel) onCancel(); 

            };

        }



        lucide.createIcons();

    </script>

    <script>

/* ======================================================

   ๐ง ALARAB 777 โ AGENT CORE (MERGED / NO UI CHANGE)

   ====================================================== */



/* ---------- NAMESPACE ISOLATION ---------- */

window.ALARAB777 = window.ALARAB777 || {};



/* ---------- CONFIG ---------- */

ALARAB777.GEMINI_MODEL = "gemini-2.5-flash";



/* placeholders ููุท โ ุงูููุงุชูุญ ูู .env */

ALARAB777.GEMINI_API_KEY = "";

ALARAB777.ELEVENLABS_API_KEY = "";

ALARAB777.VOICE_ID = "Custom_AlArab_Voice_ID";



/* ---------- MEMORY (NO CONFLICT) ---------- */

ALARAB777.MEMORY_KEY = "AlArab_777_Memory";



ALARAB777.Memory = {

    load() {

        try {

            return JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem(ALARAB777.MEMORY_KEY)) || [];

        } catch {

            return [];

        }

    },

    save(data) {

        localStorage.setItem(ALARAB777.MEMORY_KEY, JSON.stringify(data));

    },

    clear() {

        localStorage.removeItem(ALARAB777.MEMORY_KEY);

    }

};



/* ---------- STATE ---------- */

ALARAB777.chatHistory = ALARAB777.Memory.load();



/* ---------- AGENT BRAIN ---------- */

ALARAB777.Agent = {

    async ask(prompt) {

        ALARAB777.chatHistory.push({ role: "user", parts: [{ text: prompt }] });



        const payload = {

            contents: ALARAB777.chatHistory,

            systemInstruction: {

                parts: [{

                    text: "ุฃูุช ููุงู ุงูุนุฑูุงุจ 777. ุญูููุ ูุฎุชุตุฑุ ุนููู. ุญุฏ ุฃูุตู 5 ุฌูู. ุชุฎุงุทุจ ุงููุณุชุฎุฏู ูุตุฏูู."

                }]

            }

        };



        const res = await fetch(

            `https://generativelanguage.googleapis.com/v1beta/models/${ALARAB777.GEMINI_MODEL}:generateContent?key=${ALARAB777.GEMINI_API_KEY}`,

            {

                method: "POST",

                headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json" },

                body: JSON.stringify(payload)

            }

        );



        const data = await res.json();

        const reply =

            data?.candidates?.[0]?.content?.parts?.[0]?.text ||

            "ุงูุนุฑูุงุจ ูุฑู ุงูุถุจุงุจ ุงูุขูโฆ ูงูงูง";



        ALARAB777.chatHistory.push({ role: "model", parts: [{ text: reply }] });

        ALARAB777.Memory.save(ALARAB777.chatHistory);



        return reply;

    }

};



/* ---------- VOICE (HOOKED TO EXISTING PLAYER) ---------- */

ALARAB777.speak = async function (text) {

    if (

        !window.isTTSActive ||

        !ALARAB777.ELEVENLABS_API_KEY ||

        ALARAB777.VOICE_ID === "Custom_AlArab_Voice_ID"

    ) return;



    const res = await fetch(

        `https://api.elevenlabs.io/v1/text-to-speech/${ALARAB777.VOICE_ID}`,

        {

            method: "POST",

            headers: {

                "Accept": "audio/mpeg",

                "Content-Type": "application/json",

                "xi-api-key": ALARAB777.ELEVENLABS_API_KEY

            },

            body: JSON.stringify({

                text,

                model_id: "eleven_multilingual_v2"

            })

        }

    );



    const audio = await res.blob();

    ttsAudioPlayer.src = URL.createObjectURL(audio);

    ttsAudioPlayer.play();

};



/* ---------- BRIDGE WITH EXISTING UI ---------- */

/* ูุฑููุจ ุงููููู ุงูุฌุฏูุฏ ุจุฏูู ูุณุฑ handleSend ุงููุฏูู */



window._handleSend_original = window.handleSend;



window.handleSend = async function () {

    if (window.isSending) return;



    const prompt = userInput.value.trim();

    if (!prompt) return;



    addMessage(prompt, 'user');

    userInput.value = '';

    userInput.style.height = 'auto';



    setInterfaceState(true);



    try {

        const reply = await ALARAB777.Agent.ask(prompt);

        addMessage(reply, 'model');

        if (window.isTTSActive) {

            await ALARAB777.speak(reply);

        }

    } catch (e) {

        addMessage("ุฎุทุฃ ูู ููุงุฉ ุงูุนุฑูุงุจ 777.", 'system');

        console.error(e);

    }



    setInterfaceState(false);

};



/* ---------- INIT MEMORY RENDER ---------- */

window.addEventListener("load", () => {

    if (ALARAB777.chatHistory.length === 0) return;

    ALARAB777.chatHistory.forEach(m => {

        addMessage(m.parts[0].text, m.role === "user" ? "user" : "model");

    });

});

"""



โูููุง ูุนุงุฏูุฉ ุงูุฑุจุท ุงูุฌุฏูุฏุฉ ูุน ุงูุนูู ุงูุฌุฏูุฏ ุงูุฎุงุต ุจุงู ูููู ุงูุฐู ูุนูู ุนูู ููุณ ูููุงุช ุงูุฐุงูุฑุฉ ุงููุฏููุฉ ูู ุจุฅุฑุณุงูู ุฅูู ููุณ ุงููููุงุช ูุง ุชุบูุฑ ุดูุก ุ 

<script>

/* ======================================================

   ๐ง ALARAB 777 โ AGENT CORE (MERGED / NO UI CHANGE)

   ====================================================== */



/* ---------- NAMESPACE ISOLATION ---------- */

window.ALARAB777 = window.ALARAB777 || {};



/* ---------- CONFIG ---------- */

ALARAB777.GEMINI_MODEL = "gemini-2.5-flash";



/* placeholders ููุท โ ุงูููุงุชูุญ ูู .env */

ALARAB777.GEMINI_API_KEY = "";

ALARAB777.ELEVENLABS_API_KEY = "";

ALARAB777.VOICE_ID = "Custom_AlArab_Voice_ID";



/* ---------- MEMORY (NO CONFLICT) ---------- */

ALARAB777.MEMORY_KEY = "AlArab_777_Memory";



ALARAB777.Memory = {

    load() {

        try {

            return JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem(ALARAB777.MEMORY_KEY)) || [];

        } catch {

            return [];

        }

    },

    save(data) {

        localStorage.setItem(ALARAB777.MEMORY_KEY, JSON.stringify(data));

    },

    clear() {

        localStorage.removeItem(ALARAB777.MEMORY_KEY);

    }

};



/* ---------- STATE ---------- */

ALARAB777.chatHistory = ALARAB777.Memory.load();



/* ---------- AGENT BRAIN ---------- */

ALARAB777.Agent = {

    async ask(prompt) {

        ALARAB777.chatHistory.push({ role: "user", parts: [{ text: prompt }] });



        const payload = {

            contents: ALARAB777.chatHistory,

            systemInstruction: {

                parts: [{

                    text: "ุฃูุช ููุงู ุงูุนุฑูุงุจ 777. ุญูููุ ูุฎุชุตุฑุ ุนููู. ุญุฏ ุฃูุตู 5 ุฌูู. ุชุฎุงุทุจ ุงููุณุชุฎุฏู ูุตุฏูู."

                }]

            }

        };



        const res = await fetch(

            `https://generativelanguage.googleapis.com/v1beta/models/${ALARAB777.GEMINI_MODEL}:generateContent?key=${ALARAB777.GEMINI_API_KEY}`,

            {

                method: "POST",

                headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json" },

                body: JSON.stringify(payload)

            }

        );



        const data = await res.json();

        const reply =

            data?.candidates?.[0]?.content?.parts?.[0]?.text ||

            "ุงูุนุฑูุงุจ ูุฑู ุงูุถุจุงุจ ุงูุขูโฆ ูงูงูง";



        ALARAB777.chatHistory.push({ role: "model", parts: [{ text: reply }] });

        ALARAB777.Memory.save(ALARAB777.chatHistory);



        return reply;

    }

};



/* ---------- VOICE (HOOKED TO EXISTING PLAYER) ---------- */

ALARAB777.speak = async function (text) {

    if (

        !window.isTTSActive ||

        !ALARAB777.ELEVENLABS_API_KEY ||

        ALARAB777.VOICE_ID === "Custom_AlArab_Voice_ID"

    ) return;



    const res = await fetch(

        `https://api.elevenlabs.io/v1/text-to-speech/${ALARAB777.VOICE_ID}`,

        {

            method: "POST",

            headers: {

                "Accept": "audio/mpeg",

                "Content-Type": "application/json",

                "xi-api-key": ALARAB777.ELEVENLABS_API_KEY

            },

            body: JSON.stringify({

                text,

                model_id: "eleven_multilingual_v2"

            })

        }

    );



    const audio = await res.blob();

    ttsAudioPlayer.src = URL.createObjectURL(audio);

    ttsAudioPlayer.play();

};



/* ---------- BRIDGE WITH EXISTING UI ---------- */



window._handleSend_original = window.handleSend;



window.handleSend = async function () {

    if (window.isSending) return;



    const prompt = userInput.value.trim();

    if (!prompt) return;



    addMessage(prompt, 'user');

    userInput.value = '';

    userInput.style.height = 'auto';



    setInterfaceState(true);



    try {

        const reply = await ALARAB777.Agent.ask(prompt);

        addMessage(reply, 'model');

        if (window.isTTSActive) {

            await ALARAB777.speak(reply);

        }

    } catch (e) {

        addMessage("ุฎุทุฃ ูู ููุงุฉ ุงูุนุฑูุงุจ 777.", 'system');

        console.error(e);

    }



    setInterfaceState(false);

};



/* ---------- INIT MEMORY RENDER ---------- */

window.addEventListener("load", () => {

    if (ALARAB777.chatHistory.length === 0) return;

    ALARAB777.chatHistory.forEach(m => {

        addMessage(m.parts[0].text, m.role === "user" ? "user" : "model");

    });

});

</script>



ุชูุงู ูุง ุนุฑูุงุจ. **ุชู ุถุจุท ุจุฑูุชูููู โุงูุงูุญุฑุงูโ** ููุง ุทูุจุช: ุฎุจุฑู ูุตูุฑุ ูููุตู ุจุตุฑููุง ุนู ุฃุตู ุงูููุงูุ ุจูุง ุฒูุงุฏุฉ ููุง ููุตุ ููุน ุณุจุจ ูุงุถุญ.
